<(&&,(--,<(*,{#1},{#2}) --> left_of>),<(*,{#3},{#4}) --> left_of>,<(*,{#4},{#5}) --> left_of>,<(*,{#6},{#7}) --> right_of>,<(*,{#7},{#8}) --> right_of>) ==> <(*,{#5},{#9}) --> right_of>>.
<(&&,(--,<(*,{#1},{#2}) --> left_of>),<(*,{#3},{#4}) --> left_of>,<(*,{#4},{#5}) --> left_of>,<(*,{#6},{#7}) --> left_of>,<(*,{#8},{#9}) --> right_of>) ==> <(*,{#5},{#a}) --> right_of>>.
<(&&,(--,<(*,{#1},{#2}) --> below>),<(*,{#3},{#4}) --> above>,<(*,{#4},{#5}) --> above>) ==> <(*,{#5},{#6}) --> below>>.
<<(*,$1,{rect2}) --> above> <=> <(*,$1,{rect2}) --> in>>.
<(*,{rect1},[#1]) <-> above>.
<(*,{rect1},{rect2}) --> (|,(*,{rect1},[#1]),above)>.
<(*,{rect1},{rect2}) --> (&,(*,{rect1},[#1]),above)>.
<<$1 --> (*,$2,[#3])> <=> <$1 --> above>>.
<<$1 --> (*,{$2},[#3])> <=> <$1 --> above>>.
<<$1 --> (*,{rect1},[#2])> <=> <$1 --> above>>.
<<(*,$1,$2) --> (*,$1,[#3])> <=> <(*,$1,$2) --> above>>.
<<(*,{$1},$2) --> (*,{$1},[#3])> <=> <(*,{$1},$2) --> above>>.
<<(*,{rect1},$1) --> (*,{rect1},[#2])> <=> <(*,{rect1},$1) --> above>>.
<<(*,$1,{rect2}) --> (*,$1,[#2])> <=> <(*,$1,{rect2}) --> above>>.
<<(*,{$1},{rect2}) --> (*,{$1},[#2])> <=> <(*,{$1},{rect2}) --> above>>.
<(&&,(--,<(*,{#1},{#2}) --> right_of>),<(*,{#3},{#4}) --> right_of>,<(*,{#5},{#3}) --> right_of>) ==> <(*,{#6},{#4}) --> right_of>>.
<(&&,<(*,{#1},{$2}) --> in>,<(*,{#3},{$4}) --> in>,<(*,{$2},{$5}) --> in>,<(*,{$2},{$6}) --> in>,<(*,{$5},{$2}) --> in>,<(*,{$6},{$7}) --> in>,<(*,{$4},{#8}) --> in>) ==> <(*,{#9},{$7}) --> in>>.
<(&&,(--,<(*,{#1},{#2}) --> below>),<(*,{#3},{#4}) --> below>,<(*,{#5},{#6}) --> below>,<(*,{#7},{#8}) --> above>,<(*,{#8},{#9}) --> above>,<(*,{#a},{#b}) --> above>) ==> (--,<(*,{#c},{#d}) --> below>)>.
<#1 --> (|,#2,{#3})>.
<(*,[rectangle],#1) <-> right_of>.
<(*,{#1},#2) --> (|,(*,[rectangle],#2),right_of)>.
<(*,{#1},#2) --> (&,(*,[rectangle],#2),right_of)>.
<{rect2,rect3} --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})>.
<(/,left_of,_,{rect5}) --> {rect2,rect3}>.
<(/,left_of,_,{rect5}) <-> {rect2,rect3}>.
<{rect4} --> (|,(/,left_of,_,{rect5}),{rect2,rect3})>.
<{rect4} --> (&,(/,left_of,_,{rect5}),{rect2,rect3})>.
<<$1 --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})> ==> <$1 --> {rect2,rect3}>>.
<<{$1} --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})> ==> <{$1} --> {rect2,rect3}>>.
<<$1 --> {rect2,rect3}> ==> <$1 --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})>>.
<<{$1} --> {rect2,rect3}> ==> <{$1} --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})>>.
<<$1 --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})> <=> <$1 --> {rect2,rect3}>>.
<<{$1} --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})> <=> <{$1} --> {rect2,rect3}>>.
<{rect3} --> (/,left_of,_,{rect5})>.
<(&&,<(*,{#1},{#2}) --> above>,<(*,{#3},{#4}) --> above>,<(*,{#5},{#6}) --> above>,<(*,{#7},{#8}) --> below>,<(*,{#9},{#a}) --> below>) ==> <(*,{#7},{#b}) --> below>>.
<(&&,(--,<(*,{#1},{#2}) --> below>),<(*,{#3},{#4}) --> above>,<(*,{#5},{#6}) --> above>,<(*,{#7},{#8}) --> below>,<(*,{#9},{#2}) --> below>) ==> <(*,{#7},{#a}) --> below>>.
